            this._moveTotalOffset = new Phaser.Geom.Point,
            this._moveCurOffset = new Phaser.Geom.Point
        }
        reset() {
            if (Math.random() < .5)
                this._state = 0,
                this._moveStartTime = Phaser.Math.RND.integerInRange(0, N.MAX_MOVE_DELAY);
            else {
                this.setMoveProps();
                let t = .9 * Math.random();
                this._moveStartTime = Qt.timer.elapsedTime - t * this._moveTime,
                this._moveCurOffset.setTo(this._moveTotalOffset.x * t, this._moveTotalOffset.y * t),
                this._state = 1
            }
            this.respawn()
        }
        respawn() {
            let t = D.instance.spawnArea
              , e = this._members.length;
            for (; 0 != e--; )
                this._members[e].reset(t.left + Math.random() * t.width, t.top + Math.random() * t.height)
        }
        update(t) {
            let e = Qt.timer.elapsedTime
              , i = 0
              , s = 0
              , f = D.instance.spawnArea;
            if (0 == this._state)
                e >= this._moveStartTime && (this.setMoveProps(),
                this._moveStartTime = e,
                this._moveCurOffset.setTo(0, 0),
                this._state = 1);
            else {
                let t = (e - this._moveStartTime) / this._moveTime;
                t > 1 && (t = 1);
                let f = t * this._moveTotalOffset.x
                  , a = t * this._moveTotalOffset.y;
                i = f - this._moveCurOffset.x,
                s = a - this._moveCurOffset.y,
                this._moveCurOffset.x = f,
                this._moveCurOffset.y = a,
                1 == t && (this._state = 0)
            }
            let a = this._members.length
              , r = Phaser.Math.RND.integerInRange(0, 4 * a);
            for (; 0 != a--; ) {
                let e = this._members[a]
                  , n = e.bob;
                if (1 == this._state && (n.x += i * e.moveScaleX,
                n.x < f.left ? n.x = f.right : n.x > f.right && (n.x = f.left),
                n.y += s * e.moveScaleY),
                a == r) {
                    let t = e.alpha + Phaser.Math.RND.realInRange(-.15, .15);
                    t < .1 && (t = .1),
                    t > 1 && (t = 1),
                    e.alpha = t
                }
                n.alpha = t * e.alpha
            }
        }
        setMoveProps() {
            let t = Phaser.Math.DegToRad(360 * Math.random())
              , e = N.MIN_MOVE_DISTANCE + Math.random() * (N.MAX_MOVE_DISTANCE - N.MIN_MOVE_DISTANCE);
            this._moveTotalOffset.setTo(Math.cos(t) * e, -Math.sin(t) * e);
            let i = N.MIN_MOVE_SPEED + Math.random() * (N.MAX_MOVE_SPEED - N.MIN_MOVE_SPEED);
            this._moveTime = i * e
        }
    }
    N.MIN_MOVE_DELAY = 1e3,
    N.MAX_MOVE_DELAY = 2e3,
    N.MIN_MOVE_DISTANCE = 5,
    N.MAX_MOVE_DISTANCE = 15,
    N.MIN_MOVE_SPEED = 300,
    N.MAX_MOVE_SPEED = 25;

    class U {
        constructor(t) {

        }

                return this.elapsedTime;
            if (this._timeScale != this._tsTransValB) {
                let t = (this._game.loop.time - this._tsTransTimer) / this._tsTransDuration;
                t >= 1 ? (t = 1,

                this._timeScale = this._tsTransValA + (this._tsTransValB - this._tsTransValA) * t)
            }
            let t = this._game.loop.delta * this._timeScale;
            return this.delta = t / (1e3 / 60),
            this.elapsedTime += t
        }

            this._tsTransTimer = this._game.loop.time,
            this._tsTransEase = i,
            this._tsTransCompleteClbFnc = s,
            this._tsTransCompleteClbCtx = f) : (this._timeScale = t,
            this._tsTransValB = t)
        }

        }

            this._flags |= 4,

            Qt.audio && qt.instance.sys.sound.playAudioSprite("sfx", "timeRefill")
        }

            if (0 != (1 & this._flags) && this._pauseEndTime >= 0 && t >= this._pauseEndTime && (this._flags &= -2),
            0 != (2 & this._flags)) {
                let e = this._unfreezeTime - t;
                e < 1e3 && (e <= 0 ? (this._freezeFxImg.visible = !1,
                this._flags &= -3) : (this._freezeFxBlinkTimer -= Qt.timer.delta,
                this._freezeFxBlinkTimer <= 0 && (this._freezeFxBlinkTimer = 6,
                this._freezeFxImg.visible = !this._freezeFxImg.visible)))
            }
            if (0 != (4 & this._flags) && (this._bar.value < 1 ? (this._bar.value += .01,
            1 == this._bar.value && (this._refillCompleteTime = t)) : t - this._refillCompleteTime >= 1e3 && (this._bar.showIncFx = !0,
            this._flags &= -5)),
            0 == (7 & this._flags) && this._bar.value > 0) {

                e <= 0 ? qt.instance.gameOver(4) : e <= .4 && (0 == this._barOscilationState && (this._barOscilationTime = t),
                this._barOscilationState <= 0 && (this._barOscilationState = 1))
            }
            if (0 != this._barOscilationState) {
                let e = Math.sin((t - this._barOscilationTime) / 30);
                this._barOscilationState > 0 && this._bar.value >= .45 && (this._barOscilationState = -1),
                this._barOscilationState < 0 && e > 0 != this._barOscilationVal > 0 && (e = 0,
                this._barOscilationState = 0),
                this._barOscilationVal = e,
                this.updatePosition()
            }
        }
        updatePosition() {
            1 == Qt.API ? this._bar.setPosition((Qt.CAMERA_WIDTH - this._bar.width) / 2, this._camera.scrollY + 102 + 5 * this._barOscilationVal) : this._bar.setPosition(40, this._camera.scrollY + 30 + 5 * this._barOscilationVal),

        }
        handleTrunkHit(t) {
            0 == (6 & this._flags) && (0 != (1 & this._flags) && (this._flags &= -2),
            this._bar.value += this.incStep)
        }
    }

    class et {
        static decode(t) {
            et.init();
            let e, i, s, f, a, r = .75 * t.length, n = t.length, h = 0;
            "=" === t[t.length - 1] && (r--,
            "=" === t[t.length - 2] && r--);

              , o = new Uint8Array(l)

            for (e = 0; e < n; e += 4)
                i = _[t.charCodeAt(e)],
                s = _[t.charCodeAt(e + 1)],
                f = _[t.charCodeAt(e + 2)],
                a = _[t.charCodeAt(e + 3)],
                o[h++] = i << 2 | s >> 4,
                o[h++] = (15 & s) << 4 | f >> 2,
                o[h++] = (3 & f) << 6 | 63 & a;
            return l
        }
        static encode(t, e, i) {
            et.init();
            let s = new Uint8Array(t,e,i)
              , f = "";
            for (let t = 0; t < i; t += 3)
                f += et._chars[s[t] >> 2],
                f += et._chars[(3 & s[t]) << 4 | s[t + 1] >> 4],
                f += et._chars[(15 & s[t + 1]) << 2 | s[t + 2] >> 6],
                f += et._chars[63 & s[t + 2]];
            return i % 3 == 2 ? f = f.substring(0, f.length - 1) + "=" : i % 3 == 1 && (f = f.substring(0, f.length - 2) + "=="),
            f
        }
        static init() {

                et._charsLookUp = new Uint8Array(256);
                for (let t = 0; t < et._chars.length; t++)

            }

    class it {
        constructor(t) {
            this._hitTimes = [],
            this._bufView = new DataView(new ArrayBuffer(4096)),
            this._bufView.setUint8(0, it.DATA_VERSION),
            this._bufView.setUint8(5, it.GAME_UID),
            this._bufView.setUint32(16, Qt.GAME_SEED),
            this._isOpen = !1;
            let e = t.events;
            e.on(st.EVENT_RESET, this.handleReset, this),
            e.on(st.EVENT_PAUSE, this.handlePausePenalty, this),
            e.on(At.EVENT_TRUNK_HIT, this.handleTrunkHit, this)
        }
        get isOpen() {
            return this._isOpen
        }
        close(t) {
            if (!this._isOpen)
                return null;
            this._isOpen = !1,
            this._bufView.setUint16(6, Math.round(t.playTime / 1e3)),
            this._bufView.setUint32(9, t.score),
            this._bufView.setUint8(15, t.gameEndReason);
            let e = this._hitEntryBufPos;
            0 != this._hitEntryBufPosBitId && e++;
            for (const t of this._hitTimes)
                this._bufView.setUint32(e, t),
                e += 4;
            return this._bufView.setUint32(1, e),
            et.encode(this._bufView.buffer, 0, e)
        }
        handleReset() {
            this._bufView.setUint16(20, 0),
            this._isOpen = !0,
            this._hitTimes.length = 0,
            this._hitEntryBufPos = 22,
            this._hitEntryBufPosBitId = 0
        }
        handlePausePenalty(t) {
            this._isOpen && (this._bufView.setUint8(8, this._bufView.getUint8(8) + 1),
            this._bufView.setUint16(13, this._bufView.getUint16(13) + t))
        }
        handleTrunkHit(t, e, i) {
            if (i && 1 == t)
                return;
            const s = this._bufView.getUint16(20);
            this._bufView.setUint16(20, s + 1),
            0 != s && s % it.HITS_PER_TIME == 0 && this._hitTimes.push(qt.instance.playTime),
            this.addHitEntryBit(e > 0 ? 1 : 0),
            1 == t ? (this.addHitEntryBit(1),
            this.addHitEntryBit(1 != qt.instance.scoreMultiplier ? 1 : 0)) : (this.addHitEntryBit(0),
            this.addHitEntryBit(t < 0 ? 1 : 0))
        }
        addHitEntryBit(t) {
            for (; ; ) {
                let e;
                if (0 != this._hitEntryBufPosBitId) {
                    if (0 == t)
                        break;
                    e = this._bufView.getUint8(this._hitEntryBufPos)
                } else
                    e = 0;
                t && (e |= 1 << this._hitEntryBufPosBitId),
                this._bufView.setUint8(this._hitEntryBufPos, e);
                break
            }
            8 == ++this._hitEntryBufPosBitId && (this._hitEntryBufPosBitId = 0,
            this._hitEntryBufPos++)
        }
    }
    it.DATA_VERSION = 4,
    it.GAME_UID = 108,
    it.HITS_PER_TIME = 16;

            }
        }

    class ht {
        constructor() {
            this._curVals = {
                color: new Phaser.Display.Color(0,0,0,1),
                alpha: 0
            }
        }
        start(t) {
            this._settings = t,
            this._stateTime = Qt.timer.elapsedTime,
            this._state = 0;
            const e = t.color;
            this._curVals.color.setTo(e.r, e.g, e.b, 1),
            this._curVals.alpha = 0
        }
        update() {
            let t, e = Qt.timer.elapsedTime - this._stateTime;
            switch (this._state) {
            case 0:
                if (t = e / this._settings.lenIn,
                t < 1) {
                    this._curVals.alpha = this._settings.easeIn(t) * this._settings.alpha;
                    break
                }
                e -= this._settings.lenIn,
                this._stateTime += this._settings.lenIn,
                this._state++,
                this._settings.onCompleteIn && this._settings.onCompleteIn();
            case 1:
                {
                    let t = e / this._settings.lenOut;
                    if (!(t < 1))
                        return this._curVals.alpha = 0,
                        this._state++,
                        void (this._settings.onCompleteOut && this._settings.onCompleteOut());
                    this._curVals.alpha = this._settings.alpha - this._settings.easeOut(t) * this._settings.alpha;
                    break
                }
            }
            return this._curVals
        }
    }
    class lt {
        constructor(t) {
            this._scrOverlayColor = new Phaser.Display.Color,
            this._scrOverlay = new nt(t),
            this._freeFx = new M(ht,1,!0),
            this._actFx = new Phaser.Structs.List(this)
        }
        reset() {
            this._scrOverlay.enabled && (this._scrOverlay.enabled = !1,
            this._actFx.each((t=>{
                this._freeFx.returnItem(t)

            ), this),
            this._actFx.removeAll(!0))
        }
        startFx(t) {
            let e = this._freeFx.getItem();
            e.start(t),
            this._actFx.add(e),
            this._scrOverlay.enabled || (this._scrOverlay.enabled = !0)
        }
        update() {
            0 != this._actFx.length && (this._scrOverlayColor.setTo(0, 0, 0, 1),
            this._scrOverlayAlpha = 0,
            this._actFx.each((t=>{
                let e = t.update();
                if (e) {
                    e.alpha > this._scrOverlayAlpha && (this._scrOverlayAlpha = e.alpha);
                    const t = this._scrOverlayColor
                      , i = e.color
                      , s = e.alpha;
                    t.red = t.red + (i.red - t.red) * s,
                    t.green = t.green + (i.green - t.green) * s,
                    t.blue = t.blue + (i.blue - t.blue) * s
                } else
                    this._actFx.remove(t, !0),
                    this._freeFx.returnItem(t),
                    0 == this._actFx.length && (this._scrOverlay.enabled = !1)
            }
            ), this),
            this._scrOverlay.color = this._scrOverlayColor.color,
            this._scrOverlay.opacity = this._scrOverlayAlpha)
        }
    }

        }
    }
    class _t {
        constructor(t, e, i, s, f, a) {
            this._moveDistance = t,
            this._moveTime = e,
            this._moveEase = i,
            this._alphaDelay = s,
            this._alphaTime = f,
            this._alphaEase = a
        }
        get moveDistance() {
            return this._moveDistance
        }
        get moveTime() {
            return this._moveTime
        }
        get moveEase() {
            return this._moveEase
        }
        get alphaDelay() {
            return this._alphaDelay
        }
        get alphaTime() {
            return this._alphaTime
        }
        get alphaEase() {
            return this._alphaEase
        }
        updateMessage(t, e) {
            let i = 0
              , s = e.getMsgContainer()
              , f = t / this._moveTime;
            f >= 1 && (f = 1,
            i |= 1);
            let a = this._moveEase(f);
            return s.x = e.startPos.x + Math.cos(e.moveAngle) * (a * this._moveDistance),
            s.y = e.startPos.y + Math.sin(e.moveAngle) * (a * this._moveDistance),
            t > this._alphaDelay && (f = (t - this._alphaDelay) / this._alphaTime,
            f >= 1 && (f = 1,
            i |= 2),
            s.alpha = 1 - this._alphaEase(f)),
            3 != i
        }
    }

    class ut {
        constructor(t, e, i, s, f, a, r, n, h, l, o) {
            this._camera = t,
            this._dir = e,
            this._slideInTime = i,
            this._slideInEase = s,
            this._slideInAlphaStart = f,
            this._slideInAlphaEase = null == a || null == a ? s : a,
            this._slideOutTime = r,
            this._slideOutDelay = n,
            this._slideOutEase = h,
            this._slideOutAlphaEnd = l,
            this._slideOutAlphaEase = null == o || null == o ? h : o
        }
        get slideDir() {
            return this._dir
        }
        get slideInTime() {
            return this._slideInTime
        }
        get slideInEase() {
            return this._slideInEase
        }
        get slideInAlphaStart() {
            return this._slideInAlphaStart
        }
        get slideInAlphaEase() {
            return this._slideInAlphaEase
        }
        get slideOutTime() {
            return this._slideOutTime
        }
        get slideOutDelay() {
            return this._slideOutDelay
        }
        get slideOutEase() {
            return this._slideOutEase
        }
        get slideOutAlphaEnd() {
            return this._slideOutAlphaEnd
        }
        get slideOutAlphaEase() {
            return this._slideOutAlphaEase
        }
        getMessageStartX(t) {
            return this._camera.scrollX + (this._dir < 0 ? this._camera.width : -t.getMsgContainer().width)
        }
        getMessageCenterX(t) {
            return this._camera.scrollX + (this._camera.width - t.getMsgContainer().width) / 2
        }
        updateMessage(t, e) {
            let i = e.getMsgContainer()
              , s = e.state;
            switch (s) {
            case f.slideIn:
                {
                    let a = t / this._slideInTime;
                    a >= 1 && (a = 1,
                    s = f.slideOutDelay),
                    1 != this._slideInAlphaStart && (i.alpha = this._slideInAlphaStart + this._slideInAlphaEase(a) * (1 - this._slideInAlphaStart));
                    let r = this.getMessageStartX(e)
                      , n = this.getMessageCenterX(e);
                    i.x = r + this._slideInEase(a) * (n - r);
                    break
                }
            case f.slideOutDelay:
                if (t - this._slideInTime < this._slideOutDelay) {
                    i.x = this.getMessageCenterX(e);
                    break
                }
                s = f.slideOut;
            case f.slideOut:
                {
                    let a = (t - this._slideInTime - this._slideOutDelay) / this._slideOutTime;
                    a >= 1 && (a = 1,
                    s = f.completed);
                    let r = this.getMessageCenterX(e)
                      , n = this._dir < 0 ? -i.width : this._camera.width;
                    i.x = r + (n - r) * this._slideOutEase(a),
                    1 != this._slideOutAlphaEnd && (i.alpha = 1 - (1 - this._slideOutAlphaEnd) * this._slideOutAlphaEase(a));
                    break
                }
            }
            return s
        }
    }

    class xt extends Phaser.Scene {
        constructor() {
            super({

    class Ct {
        constructor() {
            let t = qt.instance;
            this._bonuses = t.add.group(),
            t.events.on(At.EVENT_BLOCK_DESTROYED, this.handleTrunkBlockDestroyed, this),
            t.events.on(At.EVENT_TRUNK_FALL, this.handleTrunkFall, this),
            t.events.on(St.EVENT_INTRO_COMPLETE, this.handleCharIntroComplete, this),
            t.events.on(Qt.EVENT_CAMERA_RESIZE, this.handleCameraResize, this)
        }
        reset() {
            this._nextBonusDelay = Ct.FIRST_BONUS_DELAY + Qt.rnd.integerInRange(Ct.BONUS_MIN_SPACING, Ct.BONUS_MAX_SPACING),
            this._bonuses.children.iterate((function(t) {
                t.reset()
            }
            ), this),
            this._mostBottomBonus = null,
            this._bonusCnt = 0,
            this._lastBonusType = 4
        }
        handleTrunkBlockDestroyed() {
            let t = At.instance;
            null != this._mostBottomBonus && this.checkBonusPickup();
            let e = It.instance.character.enabledBonuses;
            if (0 == e.length)
                return;
            if (0 == this._nextBonusDelay || It.instance.godMode || this._nextBonusDelay--,
            0 != this._nextBonusDelay)
                return;
            let i = t.getBlock(t.length - 1);
            if (0 != i.branch)
                return;
            let s, f = !1;
            if (i.blockId - 1 == t.prevBranchBlockId) {
                let e = !0;
                if (this._bonusCnt >= 3 && t.nextBranchSide == t.prevBranchSide && Qt.rnd.realInRange(0, 1) > .75 && (e = !1,
                f = !0),
                e)
                    return void t.incNextBranchDelay()
            }
            let a = Qt.rnd.integerInRange(0, e.length - 1);
            s = e[a],
            e.length > 1 && s == this._lastBonusType && (++a == e.length && (a = 0),
            s = e[a]);
            let r = this.getFreeBonus();
            r.show(s, (0 == t.nextBranchType ? Ct.LONG_BRANCH_OFFSET : Ct.SHORT_BRANCH_OFFSET) * t.nextBranchSide, t.topY - 1.4 * Q.HEIGHT + It.instance.character.branchVOffset, i.blockId),
            this._lastBonusType = s,
            null == this._mostBottomBonus && (this._mostBottomBonus = r),
            this._nextBonusDelay = Qt.rnd.integerInRange(Ct.BONUS_MIN_SPACING, Ct.BONUS_MAX_SPACING),
            f && (this._nextBonusDelay = Math.max(Math.floor(this._nextBonusDelay / 2), Ct.BONUS_MIN_SPACING)),
            this._bonusCnt++
        }
        checkBonusPickup() {
            let t = this._mostBottomBonus.blockId
              , e = At.instance.getBlock(0).blockId;
            e >= t && (It.instance.side == this._mostBottomBonus.getTrunkSide() ? (this._mostBottomBonus.pickup(),
            qt.instance.applyBonus(this._mostBottomBonus.bonusType),
            xt.instance.showPopupMsg(Ct.NAMES[this._mostBottomBonus.bonusType], this._mostBottomBonus.x, this._mostBottomBonus.y)) : e > t && this._mostBottomBonus.reset(),
            this._mostBottomBonus = this.getMostBottomBonus())
        }
        handleTrunkFall(t) {
            this._bonuses.children.iterate((function(e) {
                e.active && 0 == e.bonusState && (e.y += t)
            }
            ), this)
        }
        handleCharIntroComplete(t, e, i) {
            if (i) {
                let e = It.CHARACTERS[t].branchVOffset - It.CHARACTERS[t - 1].branchVOffset + (It.CHARACTERS[t - 1].trunkRootHeight - It.CHARACTERS[t].trunkRootHeight);
                0 != e && this._bonuses.children.iterate((function(t) {
                    t.active && 0 == t.bonusState && (t.y += e)
                }
                ), this)
            }
        }
        handleCameraResize(t) {
            this._bonuses.children.iterate((function(t) {
                t.active && (t.x = qt.CAMERA_CENTER_X + t.trunkHOffset)
            }
            ), this)
        }
        getFreeBonus() {
            let t;
            return 0 == this._bonuses.countActive(!1) ? (t = new yt(qt.instance),
            this._bonuses.add(t, !1)) : t = this._bonuses.getFirstDead(),
            t
        }
        getMostBottomBonus() {
            let t = null;
            return this._bonuses.children.iterate((function(e) {
                e.active && 0 == e.bonusState && (null == t || e.y > t.y) && (t = e)
            }
            ), this),
            t
        }

    class Pt {
        constructor() {
            this.pos = 0,
            this.len = 0
        }
        reset() {
            return this.result = null,
            this.pos = 0,
            this.len = 0,
            this.asm.reset(),
            this
        }
        process(t) {
            if (null !== this.result)
                throw new Mt("state must be reset before processing new data");
            let e = this.asm
              , i = this.heap
              , s = this.pos
              , f = this.len
              , a = 0
              , r = t.length
              , n = 0;
            for (; r > 0; )
                n = vt(i, s + f, t, a, r),
                f += n,
                a += n,
                r -= n,
                n = e.process(s, f),
                s += n,
                f -= n,
                f || (s = 0);
            return this.pos = s,
            this.len = f,
            this
        }
        finish() {
            if (null !== this.result)
                throw new Mt("state must be reset before processing new data");
            return this.asm.finish(this.pos, this.len, 0),
            this.result = new Uint8Array(this.HASH_SIZE),
            this.result.set(this.heap.subarray(0, this.HASH_SIZE)),
            this.pos = 0,
            this.len = 0,
            this
        }
    }

        function p(t, e, i, s, r) {

        function E(t, e, i, s, r, _) {
            t = t | 0;
            e = e | 0;
            i = i | 0;
            s = s | 0;
            r = r | 0;
            _ = _ | 0;

              , d = 0
              , x = 0
              , g = 0
              , p = 0

            h(s << 1);

                m(_, s, i, s, _, s) | 0
            }
        }
        return {
            sreset: r,
            salloc: n,
            sfree: h,
            z: o,
            tst: u,
            neg: _,
            cmp: c,
            add: d,
            sub: m,

    function Nt(t, e) {
        let i = t.sign
          , s = e.sign;
        i < 0 && (t = t.negate()),
        s < 0 && (e = e.negate());
        const f = t.compare(e);
        if (f < 0) {
            let f = t;
            t = e,
            e = f;
            let a = i;
            i = s,
            s = a
        }
        var a, r, n, h = Vt.ONE, l = Vt.ZERO, o = e.bitLength, _ = Vt.ZERO, c = Vt.ONE, u = t.bitLength;
        for (a = t.divide(e); (r = a.remainder) !== Vt.ZERO; )
            n = a.quotient,
            a = h.subtract(n.multiply(l).clamp(o)).clamp(o),
            h = l,
            l = a,
            a = _.subtract(n.multiply(c).clamp(u)).clamp(u),
            _ = c,
            c = a,
            t = e,
            e = r,
            a = t.divide(e);
        if (i < 0 && (l = l.negate()),
        s < 0 && (c = c.negate()),
        f < 0) {
            let t = l;
            l = c,
            c = t
        }
        return {
            gcd: e,
            x: l,
            y: c
        }
    }
    function Dt(t) {
        throw new Error("No secure random number generator available.")

    const Ft = {
        Uint32Array,
        Math
    }
      , Lt = new Uint32Array(1048576);
    let Ht;
    void 0 === Ft.Math.imul ? (Ft.Math.imul = function(t, e) {
        return t * e | 0
    }
    ,
    Ht = kt(Ft, 0, Lt.buffer),

    const Gt = new Uint32Array(0);
    class Vt {
        constructor(t) {
            let e = Gt
              , i = 0
              , s = 0;
            if (void 0 === t)
                ;
            else {
                for (var f = 0; !t[f]; f++)
                    ;
                if (i = 8 * (t.length - f),
                !i)
                    return Vt.ZERO;
                e = new Uint32Array(i + 31 >> 5);
                for (var a = t.length - 4; a >= f; a -= 4)
                    e[t.length - 4 - a >> 2] = t[a] << 24 | t[a + 1] << 16 | t[a + 2] << 8 | t[a + 3];
                f - a == 3 ? e[e.length - 1] = t[f] : f - a == 2 ? e[e.length - 1] = t[f] << 8 | t[f + 1] : f - a == 1 && (e[e.length - 1] = t[f] << 16 | t[f + 1] << 8 | t[f + 2]),
                s = 1
            }
            this.limbs = e,
            this.bitLength = i,
            this.sign = s
        }
        static fromString(t) {
            const e = function(t, e=!1) {
                for (var i = t.length, s = new Uint8Array(e ? 4 * i : i), f = 0, a = 0; f < i; f++) {
                    var r = t.charCodeAt(f);
                    if (e && 55296 <= r && r <= 56319) {
                        if (++f >= i)
                            throw new Error("Malformed string, low surrogate expected at position " + f);
                        r = (55296 ^ r) << 10 | 65536 | 56320 ^ t.charCodeAt(f)
                    } else if (!e && r >>> 8)
                        throw new Error("Wide characters are not allowed.");
                    !e || r <= 127 ? s[a++] = r : r <= 2047 ? (s[a++] = 192 | r >> 6,
                    s[a++] = 128 | 63 & r) : r <= 65535 ? (s[a++] = 224 | r >> 12,
                    s[a++] = 128 | r >> 6 & 63,
                    s[a++] = 128 | 63 & r) : (s[a++] = 240 | r >> 18,
                    s[a++] = 128 | r >> 12 & 63,
                    s[a++] = 128 | r >> 6 & 63,
                    s[a++] = 128 | 63 & r)
                }
                return s.subarray(0, a)
            }(t);
            return new Vt(e)
        }
        static fromNumber(t) {
            let e = Gt
              , i = 0
              , s = 0;
            var f = Math.abs(t);
            return f > 4294967295 ? (e = new Uint32Array(2),
            e[0] = 0 | f,
            e[1] = f / 4294967296 | 0,
            i = 52) : f > 0 ? (e = new Uint32Array(1),
            e[0] = f,
            i = 32) : (e = Gt,
            i = 0),

            Vt.fromConfig({
                limbs: e,
                bitLength: i,
                sign: s
            })
        }
        static fromArrayBuffer(t) {
            return new Vt(new Uint8Array(t))
        }
        static fromConfig(t) {

            return e.limbs = new Uint32Array(t.limbs),
            e.bitLength = t.bitLength,
            e.sign = t.sign,
            e
        }
        toString(t) {
            t = t || 16;
            const e = this.limbs
              , i = this.bitLength;
            let s = "";
            if (16 !== t)
                throw new Ot("bad radix");
            for (var f = (i + 31 >> 5) - 1; f >= 0; f--) {
                var a = e[f].toString(16);
                s += "00000000".substr(a.length),
                s += a
            }
            return s = s.replace(/^0+/, ""),
            s.length || (s = "0"),
            this.sign < 0 && (s = "-" + s),
            s
        }
        toBytes() {
            const t = this.bitLength
              , e = this.limbs;
            if (0 === t)
                return new Uint8Array(0);
            const i = t + 7 >> 3
              , s = new Uint8Array(i);
            for (let t = 0; t < i; t++) {
                let f = i - t - 1;
                s[t] = e[f >> 2] >> ((3 & f) << 3)
            }
            return s
        }
        valueOf() {
            const t = this.limbs
              , e = this.bitLength
              , i = this.sign;
            if (!i)
                return 0;
            if (e <= 32)
                return i * (t[0] >>> 0);
            if (e <= 52)
                return i * (4294967296 * (t[1] >>> 0) + (t[0] >>> 0));
            let s, f, a = 0;
            for (s = t.length - 1; s >= 0; s--)
                if (0 !== (f = t[s])) {
                    for (; 0 == (f << a & 2147483648); )
                        a++;
                    break
                }
            return 0 === s ? i * (t[0] >>> 0) : i * (1048576 * ((t[s] << a | (a ? t[s - 1] >>> 32 - a : 0)) >>> 0) + ((t[s - 1] << a | (a && s > 1 ? t[s - 2] >>> 32 - a : 0)) >>> 12)) * Math.pow(2, 32 * s - a - 52)
        }
        clamp(t) {
            const e = this.limbs;
            if (t >= this.bitLength)
                return this;
            const i = new Vt;
            let s = t + 31 >> 5
              , f = t % 32;
            return i.limbs = new Uint32Array(e.subarray(0, s)),
            i.bitLength = t,
            i.sign = this.sign,
            f && (i.limbs[s - 1] &= -1 >>> 32 - f),
            i
        }
        slice(t, e) {
            const i = this.limbs
              , s = this.bitLength;
            if (t < 0)
                throw new RangeError("TODO");
            if (t >= s)
                return Vt.ZERO;
            (void 0 === e || e > s - t) && (e = s - t);
            const f = new Vt;
            let a = t >> 5
              , r = t + e + 31 >> 5
              , n = e + 31 >> 5
              , h = t % 32
              , l = e % 32;
            const o = new Uint32Array(n);
            if (h) {
                for (var _ = 0; _ < r - a - 1; _++)
                    o[_] = i[a + _] >>> h | i[a + _ + 1] << 32 - h;
                o[_] = i[a + _] >>> h
            } else
                o.set(i.subarray(a, r));
            return l && (o[n - 1] &= -1 >>> 32 - l),
            f.limbs = o,
            f.bitLength = e,
            f.sign = this.sign,
            f
        }
        negate() {
            const t = new Vt;
            return t.limbs = this.limbs,
            t.bitLength = this.bitLength,
            t.sign = -1 * this.sign,
            t
        }
        compare(t) {
            var e = this.limbs
              , i = e.length
              , s = t.limbs
              , f = s.length;
            return this.sign < t.sign ? -1 : this.sign > t.sign ? 1 : (Lt.set(e, 0),
            Lt.set(s, i),
            Ht.cmp(0, i << 2, i << 2, f << 2) * this.sign)
        }
        add(t) {
            if (!this.sign)
                return t;
            if (!t.sign)
                return this;
            var e, i, s, f, a = this.bitLength, r = this.limbs, n = r.length, h = this.sign, l = t.bitLength, o = t.limbs, _ = o.length, c = t.sign, u = new Vt;
            i = (e = (a > l ? a : l) + (h * c > 0 ? 1 : 0)) + 31 >> 5,
            Ht.sreset();
            var d = Ht.salloc(n << 2)
              , m = Ht.salloc(_ << 2)
              , x = Ht.salloc(i << 2);
            return Ht.z(x - d + (i << 2), 0, d),
            Lt.set(r, d >> 2),
            Lt.set(o, m >> 2),
            h * c > 0 ? (Ht.add(d, n << 2, m, _ << 2, x, i << 2),
            s = h) : s = h > c ? (f = Ht.sub(d, n << 2, m, _ << 2, x, i << 2)) ? c : h : (f = Ht.sub(m, _ << 2, d, n << 2, x, i << 2)) ? h : c,
            f && Ht.neg(x, i << 2, x, i << 2),
            0 === Ht.tst(x, i << 2) ? Vt.ZERO : (u.limbs = new Uint32Array(Lt.subarray(x >> 2, (x >> 2) + i)),
            u.bitLength = e,
            u.sign = s,
            u)
        }
        subtract(t) {
            return this.add(t.negate())
        }
        square() {
            if (!this.sign)
                return Vt.ZERO;
            var t, e, i = this.bitLength, s = this.limbs, f = s.length, a = new Vt;
            e = 31 + (t = i << 1) >> 5,
            Ht.sreset();
            var r = Ht.salloc(f << 2)
              , n = Ht.salloc(e << 2);
            return Ht.z(n - r + (e << 2), 0, r),
            Lt.set(s, r >> 2),
            Ht.sqr(r, f << 2, n),
            a.limbs = new Uint32Array(Lt.subarray(n >> 2, (n >> 2) + e)),
            a.bitLength = t,
            a.sign = 1,
            a
        }
        divide(t) {
            var e, i, s = this.bitLength, f = this.limbs, a = f.length, r = t.bitLength, n = t.limbs, h = n.length, l = Vt.ZERO, o = Vt.ZERO;
            Ht.sreset();
            var _ = Ht.salloc(a << 2)
              , c = Ht.salloc(h << 2)
              , u = Ht.salloc(a << 2);
            return Ht.z(u - _ + (a << 2), 0, _),
            Lt.set(f, _ >> 2),
            Lt.set(n, c >> 2),
            Ht.div(_, a << 2, c, h << 2, u),
            (e = Ht.tst(u, a << 2) >> 2) && ((l = new Vt).limbs = new Uint32Array(Lt.subarray(u >> 2, (u >> 2) + e)),
            l.bitLength = s < e << 5 ? s : e << 5,
            l.sign = this.sign * t.sign),
            (i = Ht.tst(_, h << 2) >> 2) && ((o = new Vt).limbs = new Uint32Array(Lt.subarray(_ >> 2, (_ >> 2) + i)),
            o.bitLength = r < i << 5 ? r : i << 5,
            o.sign = this.sign),
            {
                quotient: l,
                remainder: o
            }
        }
        multiply(t) {
            if (!this.sign || !t.sign)
                return Vt.ZERO;
            var e, i, s = this.bitLength, f = this.limbs, a = f.length, r = t.bitLength, n = t.limbs, h = n.length, l = new Vt;
            i = (e = s + r) + 31 >> 5,
            Ht.sreset();
            var o = Ht.salloc(a << 2)
              , _ = Ht.salloc(h << 2)
              , c = Ht.salloc(i << 2);
            return Ht.z(c - o + (i << 2), 0, o),
            Lt.set(f, o >> 2),
            Lt.set(n, _ >> 2),
            Ht.mul(o, a << 2, _, h << 2, c, i << 2),
            l.limbs = new Uint32Array(Lt.subarray(c >> 2, (c >> 2) + i)),
            l.sign = this.sign * t.sign,
            l.bitLength = e,
            l
        }
        isMillerRabinProbablePrime(t) {
            var e = Vt.fromConfig(this)
              , i = 0;
            for (e.limbs[0] -= 1; 0 === e.limbs[i >> 5]; )
                i += 32;
            for (; 0 == (e.limbs[i >> 5] >> (31 & i) & 1); )
                i++;
            e = e.slice(i);
            for (var s = new Ut(this), f = this.subtract(Vt.ONE), a = Vt.fromConfig(this), r = this.limbs.length - 1; 0 === a.limbs[r]; )
                r--;
            for (; --t >= 0; ) {
                for (Dt(a.limbs),
                a.limbs[0] < 2 && (a.limbs[0] += 2); a.compare(f) >= 0; )
                    a.limbs[r] >>>= 1;
                var n = s.power(a, e);
                if (0 !== n.compare(Vt.ONE) && 0 !== n.compare(f)) {
                    for (var h = i; --h > 0; ) {
                        if (0 === (n = n.square().divide(s).remainder).compare(Vt.ONE))
                            return !1;
                        if (0 === n.compare(f))
                            break
                    }
                    if (0 === h)
                        return !1
                }
            }
            return !0
        }
        isProbablePrime(t=80) {
            var e = this.limbs
              , i = 0;
            if (0 == (1 & e[0]))
                return !1;
            if (t <= 1)
                return !0;
            var s = 0
              , f = 0
              , a = 0;
            for (i = 0; i < e.length; i++) {
                for (var r = e[i]; r; )
                    s += 3 & r,
                    r >>>= 2;
                for (var n = e[i]; n; )
                    f += 3 & n,
                    f -= 3 & (n >>>= 2),
                    n >>>= 2;
                for (var h = e[i]; h; )
                    a += 15 & h,
                    a -= 15 & (h >>>= 4),
                    h >>>= 4
            }
            return !!(s % 3 && f % 5 && a % 17) && (t <= 2 || this.isMillerRabinProbablePrime(t >>> 1))
        }
    }
    Vt.extGCD = Nt,
    Vt.ZERO = Vt.fromNumber(0),
    Vt.ONE = Vt.fromNumber(1);
    class Ut extends Vt {
        constructor(t) {
            if (super(),
            this.limbs = t.limbs,
            this.bitLength = t.bitLength,
            this.sign = t.sign,
            this.valueOf() < 1)
                throw new RangeError;
            if (this.bitLength <= 32)
                return;
            let e;
            if (1 & this.limbs[0]) {
                {
                    const t = 1 + (this.bitLength + 31 & -32)
                      , i = new Uint32Array(t + 31 >> 5);
                    i[i.length - 1] = 1,
                    e = new Vt,
                    e.sign = 1,
                    e.bitLength = t,
                    e.limbs = i;
                    const s = function(t, e) {
                        var i, s, f, a, r = t < 0 ? -1 : 1, n = e < 0 ? -1 : 1, h = 1, l = 0, o = 0, _ = 1;
                        for ((a = (t *= r) < (e *= n)) && (f = t,
                        t = e,
                        e = f,
                        f = r,
                        r = n,
                        n = f),
                        i = t - (s = Math.floor(t / e)) * e; i; )
                            f = h - s * l,
                            h = l,
                            l = f,
                            f = o - s * _,
                            o = _,
                            _ = f,
                            t = e,
                            e = i,
                            i = t - (s = Math.floor(t / e)) * e;
                        return l *= r,
                        _ *= n,
                        a && (f = l,
                        l = _,
                        _ = f),
                        {
                            gcd: e,
                            x: l,
                            y: _
                        }
                    }(4294967296, this.limbs[0]).y;
                    this.coefficient = s < 0 ? -s : 4294967296 - s
                }
                this.comodulus = e,
                this.comodulusRemainder = e.divide(this).remainder,
                this.comodulusRemainderSquare = e.square().divide(this).remainder
            }
        }
        reduce(t) {
            return t.bitLength <= 32 && this.bitLength <= 32 ? Vt.fromNumber(t.valueOf() % this.valueOf()) : t.compare(this) < 0 ? t : t.divide(this).remainder
        }
        inverse(t) {
            const e = Nt(this, t = this.reduce(t));
            if (1 !== e.gcd.valueOf())
                throw new Error("GCD is not 1");
            return e.y.sign < 0 ? e.y.add(this).clamp(this.bitLength) : e.y
        }
        power(t, e) {
            let i = 0;
            for (let t = 0; t < e.limbs.length; t++) {
                let s = e.limbs[t];
                for (; s; )
                    1 & s && i++,
                    s >>>= 1
            }
            let s = 8;
            e.bitLength <= 4536 && (s = 7),
            e.bitLength <= 1736 && (s = 6),
            e.bitLength <= 630 && (s = 5),
            e.bitLength <= 210 && (s = 4),
            e.bitLength <= 60 && (s = 3),
            e.bitLength <= 12 && (s = 2),
            i <= 1 << s - 1 && (s = 1),
            t = Ut._Montgomery_reduce(this.reduce(t).multiply(this.comodulusRemainderSquare), this);
            const f = Ut._Montgomery_reduce(t.square(), this)
              , a = new Array(1 << s - 1);
            a[0] = t,
            a[1] = Ut._Montgomery_reduce(t.multiply(f), this);
            for (let t = 2; t < 1 << s - 1; t++)
                a[t] = Ut._Montgomery_reduce(a[t - 1].multiply(f), this);
            const r = this.comodulusRemainder;
            let n = r;
            for (let t = e.limbs.length - 1; t >= 0; t--) {
                let i = e.limbs[t];
                for (let t = 32; t > 0; )
                    if (2147483648 & i) {
                        let e = i >>> 32 - s
                          , f = s;
                        for (; 0 == (1 & e); )
                            e >>>= 1,
                            f--;
                        for (var h = a[e >>> 1]; e; )
                            e >>>= 1,
                            n !== r && (n = Ut._Montgomery_reduce(n.square(), this));
                        n = n !== r ? Ut._Montgomery_reduce(n.multiply(h), this) : h,
                        i <<= f,
                        t -= f
                    } else
                        n !== r && (n = Ut._Montgomery_reduce(n.square(), this)),
                        i <<= 1,
                        t--
            }
            return Ut._Montgomery_reduce(n, this)
        }
        static _Montgomery_reduce(t, e) {
            const i = t.limbs
              , s = i.length
              , f = e.limbs
              , a = f.length
              , r = e.coefficient;
            Ht.sreset();
            const n = Ht.salloc(s << 2)
              , h = Ht.salloc(a << 2)
              , l = Ht.salloc(a << 2);
            Ht.z(l - n + (a << 2), 0, n),
            Lt.set(i, n >> 2),
            Lt.set(f, h >> 2),
            Ht.mredc(n, s << 2, h, a << 2, r, l);
            const o = new Vt;
            return o.limbs = new Uint32Array(Lt.subarray(l >> 2, (l >> 2) + a)),
            o.bitLength = e.bitLength,
            o.sign = 1,
            o
        }
    }

    class Yt {
        constructor() {
            this._sha = new Bt,
            this._textEncoder = new TextEncoder
        }
        hash(t) {
            let e = this._textEncoder.encode(t);
            return this._sha.reset(),
            this._sha.process(e),
            this._sha.finish(),
            Array.from(this._sha.result).map((t=>t.toString(16).padStart(2, "0"))).join("")
        }
    }
    class Xt {

            this._lastUpdateTime = -1,
            this._scoreVal = 0,
            this._scoreTime = -1
        }

            this._enabled = !1
        }
        update(t, e, i) {
            return !!this._enabled && (this._lastUpdateTime = t,
            this._scoreVal = e,
            this._scoreTime = i = Math.round(i),
            S.updateScore(e, i, this._hasher.hash(e + ":" + i + this._phrase)),
            !0)
        }
    }

        applyBonus(t) {

            ), this),

                this.pause()))
            }
            ), this))
        }
        pause() {
            this.sys.pause(),
            this._hud.sys.pause()
        }
        resume() {
            this.sys.resume(),
            this._hud.sys.resume()
        }
        reset() {
            this._arc8ScoreUpdate && this._arc8ScoreUpdate.reset(),
            this._arc8PauseCnt = 0,
            this.events.emit(st.EVENT_RESET),
            this._state = 0,
            Qt.timer.start(),

            this._remTime = Qt.curSettings.timeLimit,
            this._hud.sys.isActive() && this._hud.reset(),

        }
        handlePointerDown(t) {
            0 == this._state ? this._plHitDir = t.x < this.cameras.main.width / 2 ? 1 : -1 : 4 == this._state && this.reset()
        }
        handleResize(t, e) {
            let i = this.cameras.main;
            i.scrollY = Qt.CAMERA_MAX_HEIGHT - e,
            i.setSize(t, e),

        }
        handleGameeStart(t) {
            var e;
            5 != this._state ? (this.resume(),
            this.reset()) : this._state = 0,
            null === (e = Qt.missions) || void 0 === e || e.resetMissionProgress()
        }
        handleGameePause() {
            this.pause()
        }
        handleGameeResume() {
            this.resume();
            const t = Qt.curSettings;
            if (this._arc8PauseCnt++,
            t.freePauseCnt >= 0 && this._arc8PauseCnt > t.freePauseCnt) {
                let e = this._score;
                if (e > 0) {
                    const i = t.pausePenalty;
                    let s = 0;
                    i > e && (s = i - e),
                    this.score = Math.max(0, e - i),
                    this.events.emit(st.EVENT_PAUSE, s)
                }
            }
        }
        handleGameeMute() {
            this.sys.sound.mute = !0,
            Qt.audio = !1
        }
        handleGameeUnmute() {
            this.sys.sound.mute = !1,
            Qt.audio = !0
        }
        handleGameeSubmit() {
            this.resume(),
            this.gameOver(0)
        }
        handleGameeUseExtraLife() {
            this.resume(),
            W.instance.refill(),
            this._player.revive(),
            W.instance.pause(),
            this._hud.hideScreenOverlay(),
            this._state = 0
        }
